\section{Buddy list}

\subsection{Detailed Description}
Managing Buddies and buddy list and presence. 

{\bfseries Buddies and buddy list} ~\newline
Each buddy is represented by a \doxyref{Linphone\+Friend}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga2f0508bab6d8ded431ce8b1a679a1522} object created by function \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+new()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga6a130ccfa54cb75fc03703019c58f394}. Buddy configuration parameters like \doxyref{sip uri }{p.}{group__buddy__list_gaafd06626e9edf2c76ae85ec3351d38b2} or \doxyref{status publication }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga54ac1eb7f29193adf80f03cfffba7482} policy for this $\ast$ \doxyref{friend }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga2f0508bab6d8ded431ce8b1a679a1522} are configurable for each buddy. ~\newline
Here under a typical buddy creation\+: ~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyCode}
LinphoneFriend* my\_friend=linphone_friend_new_with_addr(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"sip:joe@sip.linphone.org"}); \textcolor{comment}{/*creates friend
       object for buddy joe*/}
linphone_friend_enable_subscribes(my\_friend,TRUE); \textcolor{comment}{/*configure this friend to emit SUBSCRIBE message after
       being added to LinphoneCore*/}
linphone_friend_set_inc_subscribe_policy(my\_friend,LinphoneSPAccept); \textcolor{comment}{/* accept Incoming subscription
       request for this friend*/}
\end{DoxyCode}
 \doxyref{friends }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga2f0508bab6d8ded431ce8b1a679a1522} status changes are reported by callback Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table.\+notify\+\_\+presence\+\_\+recv 
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} notify\_presence\_recv\_updated (\textcolor{keyword}{struct} \_LinphoneCore *lc,  
      LinphoneFriend *\textcolor{keyword}{friend}) \{
        \textcolor{keyword}{const} LinphoneAddress* friend\_address = linphone_friend_get_address(\textcolor{keyword}{friend});
        printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"New state state [%s] for user id [%s] \(\backslash\)n"}
                                ,linphone\_online\_status\_to\_string(
      linphone_friend_get_status(\textcolor{keyword}{friend}))
                                ,linphone_address_as_string (friend\_address));
\}
\end{DoxyCode}
 ~\newline
Once created a buddy can be added to the buddy list using function \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+add\+\_\+friend()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga3a8e9184320402082bf35226ae8d25b8} . Added friends will be notified about \doxyref{local status changes }{p.}{group__buddy__list_gabb6d2cac61ac420f3205a849dd59deb3} ~\newline
 Any subsequente modifications to \doxyref{Linphone\+Friend}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga2f0508bab6d8ded431ce8b1a679a1522} must be first started by a call to function \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+edit()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga254b01923c79947a5d23981d47639f40} and validated by function \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+done()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga6e28513bba28f948ee61341384a36958} 
\begin{DoxyCode}
linphone_friend_edit(my\_friend); \textcolor{comment}{/* start editing friend */}
linphone_friend_enable_subscribes(my\_friend,FALSE); \textcolor{comment}{/*disable subscription for this friend*/}
linphone_friend_done(my\_friend); \textcolor{comment}{/*commit changes triggering an UNSUBSCRIBE message*/}
\end{DoxyCode}


{\bfseries  Publishing presence status } ~\newline
Local presence status can be changed using function \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+core\+\_\+set\+\_\+presence\+\_\+model()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga8b8f1c93a0c9a7d355b1899969058fb3} .New status is propagated to all friends \doxyref{previously added }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga3a8e9184320402082bf35226ae8d25b8} to \doxyref{Linphone\+Core}{p.}{group__initializing_gaa5cf635b82dd338e7ee2dd3599d05f0a}.

{\bfseries Handling incoming subscription request} ~\newline
 New incoming subscription requests are process according to \doxyref{the incoming subscription policy state }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga54ac1eb7f29193adf80f03cfffba7482} for subscription initiated by \doxyref{members of the buddy list. }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga3a8e9184320402082bf35226ae8d25b8} ~\newline
 For incoming request comming from an unknown buddy, the call back Linphone\+Core\+V\+Table.\+new\+\_\+subscription\+\_\+request is invoked.

~\newline
 A complete tutorial can be found at \+: \doxyref{Registration tutorial}{p.}{group__buddy__tutorials}

Notifies the upper layer that a presence model change has been received for the uri or telephone number given as a parameter, by calling the appropriate callback if one has been set.

Creates a v\+Card object associated to this friend if there isn\textquotesingle{}t one yet and if the full name is available, either by the parameter or the one in the friend\textquotesingle{}s S\+IP U\+RI.

\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em name} & The full name of the friend or N\+U\+LL to use the one from the friend\textquotesingle{}s S\+IP U\+RI \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the v\+Card has been created, false if it wasn\textquotesingle{}t possible (for exemple if name and the friend\textquotesingle{}s S\+IP U\+RI are null or if the friend\textquotesingle{}s S\+IP U\+RI doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a display name), or if there is already one vcard 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+edit()}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+edit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\textbf{ Linphone\+Friend} $\ast$}]{fr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Starts editing a friend configuration. 

Because friend configuration must be consistent, applications M\+U\+ST call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+edit()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga254b01923c79947a5d23981d47639f40} before doing any attempts to modify friend configuration (such as \doxyref{address }{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga0d8802cedba64ac44cfb624026aa16f7} or \doxyref{subscription policy}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga54ac1eb7f29193adf80f03cfffba7482} and so on). Once the modifications are done, then the application must call \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+friend\+\_\+done()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga6e28513bba28f948ee61341384a36958} to commit the changes. \mbox{\label{group__buddy__list_gabb5a04025a91d8429819ca3898369bab}}

The friend will never be sent to a remote Card\+D\+AV server. Warning! Linphone\+Friends added this way will be removed on the next synchronization, and the callback contact\+\_\+deleted will be called.

Tells whether a presence model is considered online. 

It is any of theses cases\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item basic status is\textquotesingle{}open\textquotesingle{} and no activities
\item explicit \textquotesingle{}online\textquotesingle{} tag in the status 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em model} & Linphone\+Presence\+Model object \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A boolean value telling whether the presence model is considered online or not. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\label{group__buddy__list_gaafdc5ae622acaadbf1e58415756d9fa3}}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em model} & The \doxyref{Linphone\+Presence\+Model}{p.}{group__buddy__list_gad98268f00fb29b50b22b3c3da566e366} object for which to set the activity. \\

\end{DoxyReturn}
W\+A\+R\+N\+I\+NG\+: This function will modify the basic status of the model according to the activity being set. If you don\textquotesingle{}t want the basic status to be modified automatically, you can use the combination of \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+presence\+\_\+model\+\_\+set\+\_\+basic\+\_\+status()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga658e0e31786161658eb565f6724b38b3}, \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+presence\+\_\+model\+\_\+clear\+\_\+activities()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_ga0b26ab715a00173b7e4af5f3d0ac82ac} and \doxyref{linphone\+\_\+presence\+\_\+model\+\_\+add\+\_\+activity()}{p.}{group__buddy__list_gab0b32d981b0f909b8530dd577e830a0b}. \mbox{\label{group__buddy__list_ga658e0e31786161658eb565f6724b38b3}}
